\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CallAsConstructor()}{CallAsConstructor()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1MaybeLocal}{Maybe\+Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{Value}} $>$ v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Call\+As\+Constructor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Context}{Context}} $>$}]{context,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classint}{int}}}]{argc,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{Value}} $>$}]{argv\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Call an \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object}{Object}} as a constructor if a callback is set by the \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1ObjectTemplate_a1775c8f73e643c339804d2f5b628eddf}{Object\+Template\+::\+Set\+Call\+As\+Function\+Handler}} method. 

Note\+: This method behaves like the \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Function_ad9d54477a970ec3bb4a6ea69a58735de}{Function\+::\+New\+Instance}} method.

Defines a configurable, writable, enumerable property with the given value on the object unless the property already exists and is not configurable or the object is not extensible.

Returns true on success.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Maybe}{Maybe}}$<$ bool $>$ v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Define\+Own\+Property (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Context}{Context}} $>$}]{context,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{v8\+::\+Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Name}{Name}} $>$}]{key,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{v8\+::\+Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{Value}} $>$}]{value,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a05f25f935e108a1ea2d150e274602b87}{v8\+::\+Property\+Attribute}}}]{attributes = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a05f25f935e108a1ea2d150e274602b87a7ab4d58719c33b3ea2dfaefa29b111df}{None}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Implements \mbox{[}\mbox{[}Define\+Own\+Property\mbox{]}\mbox{]} for data property case, see \href{https://tc39.es/ecma262/\#table-essential-internal-methods}{\texttt{ https\+://tc39.\+es/ecma262/\#table-\/essential-\/internal-\/methods}}. 

In general, Create\+Data\+Property will be faster, however, does not allow for specifying attributes.

Returns true on success.

\index{v8::Object@{v8::Object}!DefineProperty@{DefineProperty}}
\index{DefineProperty@{DefineProperty}!v8::Object@{v8::Object}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{DefineProperty()}{DefineProperty()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Maybe}{Maybe}}$<$ bool $>$ v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Define\+Property (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Context}{Context}} $>$}]{context,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{v8\+::\+Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Name}{Name}} $>$}]{key,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1PropertyDescriptor}{Property\+Descriptor}} \&}]{descriptor }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Implements Object.\+define\+Property(\+O, P, Attributes), see \href{https://tc39.es/ecma262/\#sec-object.defineproperty}{\texttt{ https\+://tc39.\+es/ecma262/\#sec-\/object.\+defineproperty}}. 

The define\+Property function is used to add an own property or update the attributes of an existing own property of an object.

Both data and accessor descriptors can be used.

In general, Create\+Data\+Property is faster, however, does not allow for specifying attributes or an accessor descriptor.

The \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1PropertyDescriptor}{Property\+Descriptor}} can change when redefining a property.

Returns true on success.

\index{v8::Object@{v8::Object}!GetAlignedPointerFromEmbedderDataInCreationContext@{GetAlignedPointerFromEmbedderDataInCreationContext}}
\index{GetAlignedPointerFromEmbedderDataInCreationContext@{GetAlignedPointerFromEmbedderDataInCreationContext}!v8::Object@{v8::Object}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetAlignedPointerFromEmbedderDataInCreationContext()}{GetAlignedPointerFromEmbedderDataInCreationContext()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void $\ast$ v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Get\+Aligned\+Pointer\+From\+Embedder\+Data\+In\+Creation\+Context (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{v8\+::\+Isolate}} $\ast$}]{isolate,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classint}{int}}}]{index }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the context in which the object was created (see \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_ac5b955080a33fa56f2b38052532a5a6b}{Get\+Creation\+Context()}}) and if it\textquotesingle{}s available reads respective embedder field value. 

If the context can\textquotesingle{}t be obtained nullptr is returned. Basically it\textquotesingle{}s a shortcut for obj-\/$>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_ac5b955080a33fa56f2b38052532a5a6b}{Get\+Creation\+Context()}}.Get\+Aligned\+Pointer\+From\+Embedder\+Data(index) which doesn\textquotesingle{}t create a handle for \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Context}{Context}} object on the way and doesn\textquotesingle{}t try to expand the embedder data attached to the context. In case the \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local$<$\+Context$>$}} is already available because of other reasons, it\textquotesingle{}s fine to keep using \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Context_a4339a06a2e0c87454c15c6dada37164f}{Context\+::\+Get\+Aligned\+Pointer\+From\+Embedder\+Data()}}.

Prefer using version with \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}} parameter if you have an \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}}, otherwise use the other one.

Gets a 2-\/byte-\/aligned native pointer from an internal field. 

This field must have been set by Set\+Aligned\+Pointer\+In\+Internal\+Field, everything else leads to undefined behavior.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classint}{int}} v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Get\+Identity\+Hash (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns the identity hash for this object. 

The current implementation uses a hidden property on the object to store the identity hash.

The return value will never be 0. Also, it is not guaranteed to be unique.

\index{v8::Object@{v8::Object}!GetInternalField@{GetInternalField}}
\index{GetInternalField@{GetInternalField}!v8::Object@{v8::Object}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetInternalField()}{GetInternalField()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Data}{Data}} $>$ v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Get\+Internal\+Field (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classint}{int}}}]{index }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Gets the data from an internal field. 

To cast the return value into \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{v8\+::\+Value}} subtypes, it needs to be casted to a \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{v8\+::\+Value}} first. For example, to cast it into \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1External}{v8\+::\+External}}\+:

object-\/$>$Get\+Internal\+Field(index).As$<$v8\+::\+Value$>$().As$<$v8\+::\+External$>$();

The embedder should make sure that the internal field being retrieved using this method has already been set with \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_ac58ef882458d9596ce2a596341d53323}{Set\+Internal\+Field()}} before.

Gets the property attributes of a property which can be None or any combination of Read\+Only, Dont\+Enum and Dont\+Delete. 

Returns None when the property doesn\textquotesingle{}t exist.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1MaybeLocal}{Maybe\+Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Array}{Array}} $>$ v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Get\+Property\+Names (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Context}{Context}} $>$}]{context }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns an array containing the names of the enumerable properties of this object, including properties from prototype objects. 

The array returned by this method contains the same values as would be enumerated by a for-\/in statement over this object.

Interceptors in the prototype chain are not called.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Object_a548a8d4329cf890be3698f1bff9b9837}\label{classv8_1_1Object_a548a8d4329cf890be3698f1bff9b9837}} 
\index{v8::Object@{v8::Object}!Has@{Has}}
\index{Has@{Has}!v8::Object@{v8::Object}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Has()}{Has()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Maybe}{Maybe}}$<$ bool $>$ v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Has (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Context}{Context}} $>$}]{context,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{Value}} $>$}]{key }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_a548a8d4329cf890be3698f1bff9b9837}{Object\+::\+Has()}} calls the abstract operation Has\+Property(\+O, P), see \href{https://tc39.es/ecma262/\#sec-hasproperty}{\texttt{ https\+://tc39.\+es/ecma262/\#sec-\/hasproperty}}. 

\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_a548a8d4329cf890be3698f1bff9b9837}{Has()}} returns true, if the object has the property, either own or on the prototype chain. Interceptors, i.\+e., Property\+Query\+Callbacks, are called if present.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_a548a8d4329cf890be3698f1bff9b9837}{Has()}} has the same side effects as Java\+Script\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily variable in object}. For example, calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_a548a8d4329cf890be3698f1bff9b9837}{Has()}} on a revoked proxy will throw an exception.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_a548a8d4329cf890be3698f1bff9b9837}{Has()}} converts the key to a name, which possibly calls back into Java\+Script.
\end{DoxyNote}
See also \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_acfe461c8e81a3d078d62ece594cb1994}{v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Has\+Own\+Property()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_a243e282f3c395f8eaf465d5bd4139017}{v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Has\+Real\+Named\+Property()}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Object_a243e282f3c395f8eaf465d5bd4139017}\label{classv8_1_1Object_a243e282f3c395f8eaf465d5bd4139017}} 
\index{v8::Object@{v8::Object}!HasRealNamedProperty@{HasRealNamedProperty}}
\index{HasRealNamedProperty@{HasRealNamedProperty}!v8::Object@{v8::Object}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{HasRealNamedProperty()}{HasRealNamedProperty()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Maybe}{Maybe}}$<$ bool $>$ v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Has\+Real\+Named\+Property (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Context}{Context}} $>$}]{context,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Name}{Name}} $>$}]{key }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Use \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_a243e282f3c395f8eaf465d5bd4139017}{Has\+Real\+Named\+Property()}} if you want to check if an object has an own property without causing side effects, i.\+e., without calling interceptors. 

This function is similar to \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_acfe461c8e81a3d078d62ece594cb1994}{v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Has\+Own\+Property()}}, but it does not call interceptors.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Consider using non-\/masking interceptors, i.\+e., the interceptors are not called if the receiver has the real named property. See {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_af4789f0aeb8680e353901a35810cac1aa8678eef5728c64ca2122dfe336f116aa}{v8\+::\+Property\+Handler\+Flags\+::k\+Non\+Masking}}}.
\end{DoxyNote}
See also \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_a548a8d4329cf890be3698f1bff9b9837}{v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Has()}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classv8_1_1Object_a959a080377dcc1f1fe8aa92c36c3e3e0}\label{classv8_1_1Object_a959a080377dcc1f1fe8aa92c36c3e3e0}} 
\index{v8::Object@{v8::Object}!IsApiWrapper@{IsApiWrapper}}
\index{IsApiWrapper@{IsApiWrapper}!v8::Object@{v8::Object}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{IsApiWrapper()}{IsApiWrapper()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Is\+Api\+Wrapper (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}



Returns true if this object can be generally used to wrap object objects. 

This means that the object either follows the convention of using embedder fields to denote type/instance pointers or is using the \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_a657610a5db05d2673cb8c4ad855a1c6e}{Wrap()}}/\+Unwrap() APIs for the same purpose. Returns false otherwise.

Note that there may be other objects that use embedder fields but are not used as API wrapper objects. E.\+g., \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Promise}{v8\+::\+Promise}} may in certain configuration use embedder fields but promises are not generally supported as API wrappers. The method will return false in those cases.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object}{v8\+::\+Object}} $>$ v8\+::\+Object\+::\+New (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}} $\ast$}]{isolate,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{Value}} $>$}]{prototype\+\_\+or\+\_\+null,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Name}{Name}} $>$ $\ast$}]{names,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{Value}} $>$ $\ast$}]{values,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{length }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



Creates a Java\+Script object with the given properties, and a the given prototype\+\_\+or\+\_\+null (which can be any Java\+Script value, and if it\textquotesingle{}s null, the newly created object won\textquotesingle{}t have a prototype at all). 

This is similar to Object.\+create(). All properties will be created as enumerable, configurable and writable properties.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1MaybeLocal}{Maybe\+Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1String}{String}} $>$ v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Object\+Proto\+To\+String (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Context}{Context}} $>$}]{context }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Call builtin Object.\+prototype.\+to\+String on this object. 

This is different from \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value_a9a3128213e673903645cca6fa03c8f0c}{Value\+::\+To\+String()}} that may call user-\/defined to\+String function. This one does not.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{PreviewEntries()}{PreviewEntries()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1MaybeLocal}{v8\+::\+Maybe\+Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Array}{v8\+::\+Array}} $>$ v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Preview\+Entries (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool $\ast$}]{is\+\_\+key\+\_\+value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



If this object is a \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Set}{Set}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Map}{Map}}, Weak\+Set or Weak\+Map, this returns a representation of the elements of this object as an array. 

If this object is a Set\+Iterator or Map\+Iterator, this returns all elements of the underlying collection, starting at the iterator\textquotesingle{}s current position. For other types, this will return an empty Maybe\+Local$<$\+Array$>$ (without scheduling an exception).

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SetAlignedPointerInInternalField()}{SetAlignedPointerInInternalField()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Set\+Aligned\+Pointer\+In\+Internal\+Field (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classint}{int}}}]{index,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets a 2-\/byte-\/aligned native pointer in an internal field. 

To retrieve such a field, Get\+Aligned\+Pointer\+From\+Internal\+Field must be used, everything else leads to undefined behavior.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Maybe}{Maybe}}$<$ bool $>$ v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Set\+Lazy\+Data\+Property (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Context}{Context}} $>$}]{context,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{v8\+::\+Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Name}{Name}} $>$}]{name,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a1140451638664254f72f51ad3071fe7d}{Accessor\+Name\+Getter\+Callback}}}]{getter,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{v8\+::\+Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{Value}} $>$}]{data = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{Local}}$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Value}{Value}}$>$()},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a05f25f935e108a1ea2d150e274602b87}{Property\+Attribute}}}]{attributes = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a05f25f935e108a1ea2d150e274602b87a7ab4d58719c33b3ea2dfaefa29b111df}{None}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a29711319c2b9fc7716d65faee2f7b9cb}{Side\+Effect\+Type}}}]{getter\+\_\+side\+\_\+effect\+\_\+type = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a29711319c2b9fc7716d65faee2f7b9cba990e9e01ed66f6917a426b610d20ac46}{Side\+Effect\+Type\+::k\+Has\+Side\+Effect}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a29711319c2b9fc7716d65faee2f7b9cb}{Side\+Effect\+Type}}}]{setter\+\_\+side\+\_\+effect\+\_\+type = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a29711319c2b9fc7716d65faee2f7b9cba990e9e01ed66f6917a426b610d20ac46}{Side\+Effect\+Type\+::k\+Has\+Side\+Effect}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Attempts to create a property with the given name which behaves like a data property, except that the provided getter is invoked (and provided with the data value) to supply its value the first time it is read. 

After the property is accessed once, it is replaced with an ordinary data property.

Analogous to \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Template_ab306ba858f4e71a25ebba4380ea5791f}{Template\+::\+Set\+Lazy\+Data\+Property}}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classT}{T}} $\ast$ v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Unwrap (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{v8\+::\+Isolate}} $\ast$}]{isolate,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{v8\+::\+Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object}{v8\+::\+Object}} $>$ \&}]{wrapper }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}



Unwraps a JS wrapper object. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em tag} & The tag for retrieving the wrappable instance. Must match the tag that has been used for a previous {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_a657610a5db05d2673cb8c4ad855a1c6e}{Wrap()}}} operation. \\
\hline
{\em isolate} & The \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}} for the {\ttfamily wrapper} object. \\
\hline
{\em wrapper} & The JS wrapper object that should be unwrapped. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the C++ wrappable instance, or nullptr if the JS object has never been wrapped. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Wrap()}{Wrap()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [11/16]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$Cpp\+Heap\+Pointer\+Tag tag$>$ \\
Use Wrap with \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_1_1Wrappable}{Wrappable}}$\ast$ wrappable static \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacev8_a0bef2ddcea6f8ab8f2a79ab80c2a64f7}{instead}} void v8\+::\+Object\+::\+Wrap (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{v8\+::\+Isolate}} $\ast$}]{isolate,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Local}{v8\+::\+Local}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object}{v8\+::\+Object}} $>$ \&}]{wrapper,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{wrappable }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}



Wraps a JS wrapper with a C++ instance. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em tag} & The pointer tag that should be used for storing this object. Future {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Object_ac9812adb53766f0410d3275c53b49cfa}{Unwrap()}}} operations must provide a matching tag. \\
\hline
{\em isolate} & The \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1Isolate}{Isolate}} for the {\ttfamily wrapper} object. \\
\hline
{\em wrapper} & The JS wrapper object. \\
\hline
{\em wrappable} & The C++ object instance that is wrapped by the JS object. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
